NOTICE

CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE

K. Rajesh a male child born to Thiru V. Kuppuswamy on 25th May 1992 residing at No. 1‘X’-Block, R.V. Nagar,
Jafferkhan Pet, Chennai-600 083, has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery by Dr.V.
Jayaraman Ms,Mch,MNAMS, Dip.N.B,PhD.,FICS Professor and Head Department of Burns, Plastic & Reconstructives
Surgery, Kilpauk Medical College Hospital, Chennai-600 010, By this I, may be treated as a female and shall henceforth be
known as K. RAGAVI.

Chennai,
